<script>
    (function(){
        function queryString(name){
            //get url query params
            var reg = new RegExp('(^|&)' + name + '=([^&]*)(&|$)', 'i')
            var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg)
            if (r != null) return unescape(r[2])
            return null
        }
        var setCookie =  function(name, val, expires, domain) {
            /*setCookie start*/
            var __CurrentMainDomain__ = (function() {
                var hostnameArray = location.hostname.split('.')
                return '.' + hostnameArray.slice(1).join('.')
            })()

            //domain = domain || __CurrentMainDomain__;
            var text = String(encodeURIComponent(val))
            var date = new Date()
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + Number(expires) * 1000)
            text += '; expires=' + date.toUTCString()
            // domain
            text += '; path=/'
            if (typeof domain != 'undefined' && domain != '') {
                text += '; domain=' + __CurrentMainDomain__
            }

            document.cookie = name + '=' + text
        }  
        function set_uk_jump_cookie() {
            var p_from_country = queryString("from_country");
            var is_manual_change_site = queryString("is_manual_change_site");
            var isFromOriginBtn = queryString('is_from_origin_btn')
            var jump_to_all = ['uk', 'in', 'mx', 'hk', 'tw', 'vn', 'se'];
            if (is_manual_change_site == 0) { // 程序内切换
                setCookie('is_manual_change_site', 0, undefined, 'shein.com')
            }
            if(jump_to_all.indexOf(p_from_country) > -1 && isFromOriginBtn == 0){  //跨域回跳
                setCookie("jump_to_"+p_from_country, "0", 3600 * 24, 1)
            }
        }
        set_uk_jump_cookie()
    })()
</script>

    ;(function (_win, _doc, _src, _fun, _script, _scriptBef) {
        if(typeof _win[_fun] != 'function'){
            _win[_fun] = function () {
                if(!_win[_fun].waitingCommands){
                    _win[_fun].waitingCommands = []
                }
                _win[_fun].waitingCommands.push(arguments)
            };

      (i[r].q = i[r].q || []).push(arguments)
    }, i[r].l = 1 * new Date();

  function GB_ga_getCookie(name){
    var value = "; " + document.cookie;
    var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
    if (parts.length >= 2) {
      return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
    } else {
      return ''
    }
  }
  function dateFormat(fmt, d) {
    const o = {
      'M+': d.getMonth() + 1, // 月份
      'd+': d.getDate(), // 日
      'h+': d.getHours(), // 小时
      'm+': d.getMinutes(), // 分
      's+': d.getSeconds(), // 秒
      'q+': Math.floor((d.getMonth() + 3) / 3), // 季度
      S: d.getMilliseconds() // 毫秒
    }
    if (/(y+)/.test(fmt)) fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (d.getFullYear() + '').substr(4 - RegExp.$1.length))
    for (var k in o) if (new RegExp('(' + k + ')').test(fmt)) fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, RegExp.$1.length == 1 ? o[k] : ('00' + o[k]).substr(('' + o[k]).length))
    return fmt
  }

  var _gaGetQueryString = function(name) {
    //get url query params
    var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)", "i");
    var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
    if (r != null) return unescape(r[2]); return null;
  }

  function GBGaSend(params) {
    var payload = [GB_ANALYSIS_GA_SEND, 'event']
    for (var key in params) {
      if (typeof params[key] !== 'undefined') {
        payload.push(params[key])
      }
      if (key == 'beacon') {
        payload.push({ transport: 'beacon' })
      }
    }
    ga.apply(null, payload)
  }

    var regex

    function update () {
      regex = new RegExp('(' + list.join('|') + ')', 'i')
    }

    window.isbot = function (userAgent) {
      return regex.test(userAgent)
    }

    try {
      // Address: Cubot browser
      // Risk: Uses lookbehind assertion
      new RegExp('(?<! cu)bot').test('dangerbot')
      list.splice(list.lastIndexOf('bot'), 1)
      list.push('(?<! cu)bot')
      list.splice(list.lastIndexOf('search'), 1)
      list.push('(?<! (ya|yandex))search')
    } catch (error) {
      // ignore errors
    }

    update()

    window.isClientBot = false
    try {
      window.isClientBot = isbot(navigator.userAgent)
    } catch (e) {}
  })();

    <script>
    // 环境变量 localhost/debug/gray/production
    var NODE_SERVER_ENV = 'production';

    var ErrorJs = (function(global) {
        if(global.ErrorJs) return global.ErrorJs;

        var _errorMap = {}; // 存储错误id，判断是否是重复上报
        var _config = {
            id: 0, // id, 若没有id不会上报
            url: 'https://www.srmdata.com/unusual', // 上报 接口
            ignore: [], // 忽略某个错误, 支持 Regexp 和 Function
            random: 1, // 抽样 0-1 1为全量
            delay: 1000, // 延迟上报
            repeat: 5, // 重复上报次数(对于同一个错误超过多少次不上报),
            hostnameFilter: ['shein.com', 'shein.co', 'shein.in', 'shein.tw', 'shein.se', 'sheinoutlet.com', 'emmacloth.com', 'makemechic.com', 'romwe.com', 'romwe.co'],
            envFilter: ['localhost', 'debug', 'gray']
        };

        var E = {
            extend: function(target, source) {
                for(var key in source) {
                    target[key] = source[key];
                }
                return target;
            },
            isObject: function(value) {
                return Object.prototype.toString.call(value) === '[object Object]';
            },
            checkType: function(value, type) {
                return Object.prototype.toString.call(value) === '[object ' + type + ']';
            },
            // 判断重复次数是否超过配置的次数
            isRepeat: function(id) {
                if(!id) return false;
                var times = _errorMap[id] = (parseInt(_errorMap[id], 10) || 0) + 1;
                return times > _config.repeat;
            },
            isRandomPassed: function() {
                return Math.random() >= _config.random;
            },
            // 根据ignore配置项过滤掉不需要上报的错误
            shouldIgnore: function(msg) {
                var ignoreConf = _config.ignore;
                return ignoreConf.some(function(value) {
                    return (E.checkType(value, 'RegExp') && value.test(msg)) || (E.checkType(value, 'Function') && value(msg));
                })
            },
            filterEnvAndHost: function() {
                var hostname = '';
                if(global.location) hostname = global.location.hostname;
                // 本地/测试/灰度环境不上报，不在监控域名内的不上报
                var envPass = _config.envFilter.indexOf(NODE_SERVER_ENV) === -1;
                var hostPass = _config.hostnameFilter.some(function(host) {
                    return hostname.indexOf(host) > -1;
                });

                return  envPass && hostPass;
            }
        }

        // 重写onerror方法
        var orgError = global.onerror;
        global.onerror = function(msg, url, row, col, error) {
            var _id = msg + ',' + row + ',' + col;
            var errorObj = {
                msg: msg,
                url: url,
                row: row,
                col: col,
                error: error,
                _id: _id
            }
            if(_config.id) {
                report.filterError(errorObj)
            }
            orgError && orgError.apply(global, arguments);
        }

        var report = global.ErrorJs = {
            // 初始化
            init: function(config) {
                if(E.isObject(config)) {
                    _config = E.extend(_config, config);
                }
                return report;
            },
            sendError: function(errorType, url, data) {
                data = E.extend(data, report.extraParams);
                if(global.sa) {
                    global.sa(errorType, url, data);
                }
            },
            filterError: function(errorObj) {
                if (typeof window.isClientBot !== 'undefined' && window.isClientBot) return

                var errorBaseData = {
                    page_type: '',
                    browser_ua: '',
                    client_url: errorObj.url,
                    error_type: 'script_error',
                    error_data: errorObj.msg,
                    error_col: errorObj.col,
                    error_row: errorObj.row,
                    error_stack: errorObj.error && errorObj.error.stack || '',
                }
                if(E.shouldIgnore(errorObj.msg)) return;
                if(E.isRepeat(errorObj._id)) return;
                if(E.isRandomPassed()) return;
                if(!E.filterEnvAndHost()) return;

                report.sendError('error', _config.url, errorBaseData);
            },
            extraParams: {
                page_type: '', // 页面类型
                page_type_detail: '' // 页面类型详情
            },

            __onerror__: orgError
        }

        return report;
    }(window))

    var ignoreArr = [/Script error/i, /\$ is not defined/i, /Vue is not defined/i, /transformImg/i, /UET/, /"Vue" is not defined/i];

    ErrorJs.init({
        id: 1,
        url: 'https://www.srmdata.com/unusual',
        ignore: ignoreArr,
        random: 1,
        repeat: 1,
    })

    ErrorJs.extraParams.page_type = window.pageTypeForMonitor || 'other';
</script>

    var loadingStartTime = new Date().getTime();
    function getServerUrl() {
        var environment = 'production';
        var url = '';
        switch(environment) {
            case 'gray':
                url = 'https://api-sensors.shein.com/sa?project=project_gray'
                break
            case 'production':
                url = 'https://api-sensors.shein.com/sa?project=production'
                break
            default:
                url = 'https://api-sensors.shein.com/sa?project=default'
                break
        }
        return url
    }
    function getCookie(name) {
        var value = "; " + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
        if (parts.length >= 2) {
            return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
        } else {
            return undefined;
        }
    }
    function getShowLog() {
        // sensor-analysisi-show-log  2 展示 3 隐藏 
        // 0 根据环境变量判断
        var tag = 0
        var result = 0
        try {
            tag = sessionStorage.getItem('sensor-analysisi-show-log') || getCookie('sensor-show-log') || 0
        } catch(e) {}
        switch (Number(tag)) {
            case 2:
                result = true
                break
            case 3:
                result = false
                break
            case 0:
                // result = 'production' === 'production' ? false : true
                resule = false
                break
        }
        return result
    }

        var S_Module = S_Module || {};
        (function(){
            var modules = {};
            //定义
            S_Module.define = function(name, obj){
                modules[name] = obj;
            };
            //引用模块
            S_Module.require = function(name){
                if( modules[name] )
                return modules[name];
                // else
                // console.error('模块 ' + name + ' 加载失败');
            };
            S_Module.initModule = function(arr, opts){
                opts = opts || {};
                for( var i=0; i<arr.length; i++ ){
                    var name = arr[i];
                    var module = modules[name];
                    if( module ){
                        module.initialize && module.initialize(opts);
                    } else {
                        // console.error('模块 ' + name + ' 加载失败');
                    }
                }
            };
        })();
    </script>

<script>
    var gbExposeTraceid
    ;!function() {
        var traceidComponents = {}

        //购物流程 traceid 追踪
        gbExposeTraceid = function(type, payload) {
            try {
                var traceids = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('saTraceids'))

                if(!traceids) {
                    traceids = {}
                }
                var defaultTraceid = 'spc`' + Date.now() + '`'+ (window.gbGetCookie('cookieId') || '')
                var traceid =''
                if(type == 'setComponent') {
                    if(!traceidComponents[payload.componentName]) {
                        traceid = payload.traceid || defaultTraceid
                        if(payload.params){
                            traceid +='`'+payload.params
                        }
                        traceidComponents[payload.componentName] = traceid
                    }else{
                        traceid = traceidComponents[payload.componentName]
                    }
                } else if(type == 'getComponent') {
                    if(!traceidComponents[payload.componentName]){
                        traceidComponents[payload.componentName] = defaultTraceid
                    }
                    traceid = traceidComponents[payload.componentName]
                } else if(type == 'setProduct') {
                    traceid = payload.traceid || defaultTraceid
                    if(payload.params){
                        traceid +='`'+payload.params
                    }
                    traceids[payload.goods_id] = traceid
                } else if(type == 'getProduct') {
                    if(!traceids[payload.goods_id]){
                      traceids[payload.goods_id] = defaultTraceid
                    }
                    traceid = traceids[payload.goods_id]
                }
                sessionStorage.setItem('saTraceids', JSON.stringify(traceids))
                return traceid
            } catch (error) {
                console.log(error);
            }
        }
    }();
    var gbAddBagTraceFrom
    ;!function() {
        //追踪加车来源
        gbAddBagTraceFrom = function(type, payload) {
            var tracefrom = null
            var addBagFrom = ''
            try {
                tracefrom = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('saAddBagTraceFrom')) || {}
                if(type == 'setProductFrom') {
                    tracefrom[payload.goods_id] = payload.from || 'other'
                } else if(type == 'getProductFrom') {
                    addBagFrom = tracefrom[payload.goods_id] || 'other'
                }
                sessionStorage.setItem('saAddBagTraceFrom', JSON.stringify(tracefrom))
                return addBagFrom
            } catch (error) {
                console.log(error);
            }
        }
    }();
    var gbGetCookie = function(name) {
        var value = "; " + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
        if (parts.length >= 2) {
            return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
        } else {
            return undefined;
        }
    }

    var gbGetQueryString = function(name) {
        //get url query params
        var reg = new RegExp('(^|&)' + name + '=([^&]*)(&|$)', 'i')
        var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg)
        if (r != null) return unescape(r[2])
        return null
    }
    window.gbExposeTraceid = gbExposeTraceid
    window.gbGetCookie = gbGetCookie
    window.gbGetQueryString = gbGetQueryString
    window.gbAddBagTraceFrom = gbAddBagTraceFrom
</script>

<script>
    (function() {
        var setCookie = function(name, val, expires, domain) {
            /*setCookie start*/
            var __CurrentMainDomain__ = (function() {
                var hostnameArray = location.hostname.split('.')
                return '.' + hostnameArray.slice(-2).join('.')
            })()

            //domain = domain || __CurrentMainDomain__;
            var text = String(encodeURIComponent(val))
            var date = new Date()
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + Number(expires) * 1000)
            text += '; expires=' + date.toUTCString()
            // domain
            text += '; path=/'
            if (typeof domain != 'undefined' && domain != '') {
                text += '; domain=' + __CurrentMainDomain__
            }

            document.cookie = name + '=' + text
        }
        var getCookie = function(name) {
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length >= 2) {
                return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
            } else {
                return undefined;
            }
        }
        if (location.pathname == '/') {
            setCookie('cate_active_name', 0, 3600 * 24 * 30)
            setCookie('cate_channel_type', document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-0').dataset.channel_type, 3600 * 24 * 30)
        }
        var cate_active_name = getCookie('cate_active_name')
        document.querySelector('.j-nav2-ctn-holder').style.display = 'none'

        if (cate_active_name && document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-' + cate_active_name) && document.querySelector('.j-nav2-ctn-' + cate_active_name)) {

            document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-' + cate_active_name).className += ' cate-active'
            document.querySelector('.j-nav2-ctn-' + cate_active_name).style.display = 'table-cell'
            setCookie('cate_channel_type', document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-' + cate_active_name).dataset.channel_type, 3600 * 24 * 30)

        } else if (document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-0') && document.querySelector('.j-nav2-ctn-0')) {

            document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-0').className += ' cate-active'
            document.querySelector('.j-nav2-ctn-0').style.display = 'table-cell'
            setCookie('cate_channel_type', document.querySelector('.j-nav-first-cate-0').dataset.channel_type, 3600 * 24 * 30)

        }
    })()
</script>

          getCustomerChannel: function() {
            var self = this;
            $.get('/getCustomerChannel', function(res) {
              self.showSustomer = true;//接口如果错误展示默认
              if(res && res.code == 0 && res.info && res.info.entrance && res.info.entrance.navigationBar && res.info.entrance.navigationBar.open == 0) {
                self.showSustomer = false; //请求成功未发布不显示
              }
              if(res && res.code == 0 && res.info && res.info.pageDesc && res.info.pageDesc.length){

                var preRobotLoginInter = setInterval(function(){
                  if(typeof preRobotLogin != 'undefined'){
                    preRobotLogin.loginModalText = res.info.pageDesc[0]
                    clearInterval(preRobotLoginInter)
                  }
                }, 500)


              }
              if( res && res.code == 0 && res.info && res.info.desc ){
                  var desc = res.info.desc;
                  var descLen = desc.length;
                  for( var i = 0; i < descLen;i++ ){
                      if(desc[i].channelName === 'ContactCustomerService'){
                          self.lang_footer_customer = desc[i].title;
                          self.SHEIN_PC_KEY_4097 = desc[i].content;
                      }
                  }
              }
            })
          },
          openRobot: function() {
            $.ajax({
              type: 'POST',
              url: '/user/auth/getUserInfo',
              async: false,
              success: function(res) {
                var pageName = "navigationBar";
                if(typeof SaPageInfo != "undefined") {
                  if(SaPageInfo.page_name == 'page_order_list'){
                    pageName = "orderListPage"
                  }else if(SaPageInfo.page_name == 'page_order_detail'){
                    pageName = "orderDetailPage"
                  }else if(SaPageInfo.page_name == 'page_checkout'){
                    pageName = "checkoutPage"
                  }else if(SaPageInfo.page_name == 'page_goods_detail'){
                    pageName = "productDetailPage"
                  }

                }

                  if (res.username != null) {
                     //跳转客服机器人页面
                     window.open(location.origin+'/robot?page=navigationBar')
                  } else {

                    preRobotLogin.loginModalShow()
                    window.LOGIN_GA_POPUPS_SEND({ scenes: 'livechat' })
                    // onlineHelpLoginPopGA({action:"PopUps",label:"Sign-ClickLiveChat"})
                  }

                  if(typeof SaPageInfo == "undefined"){
                    SaPageInfo = {
                      page_id: 0,
                      page_name:'page_other',
                      page_param: {},
                    };
                  }
                  sa('send',{
                    'activity_name':'click_support',
                    activity_param: {
                        'type': 'customer_service'
                    },
                  })
                }
              }
            })
            GBGaSend({

                label: '导航栏'
            })
          },

        // 快速注册弹窗
        function getCookie(name) {//取最新的cookie
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length >= 2) {
                return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
            } else {
                return undefined;
            }
        }
        function checkSameCookie(objName){
          var arrStr = document.cookie.split("; "),count=0;
          for (var i = 0; i < arrStr.length; i++) {
            var temp = arrStr[i].split("=");
            if (temp[0] == objName) {
              count++
            }
          }
          return count>1;
        }

            SHEIN_W.setCookie('currency', currency, 3600 * 24)

          // 免邮信息
          $.get('/product/shippingDetail', function(shippingData){
              var freeHTML = [];
              if(shippingData && shippingData.length){
                  var freeShippingTipsData = [];
                  var textTpl = {
                    express_shipping: "&lt;storng style=&#34;text-transform: capitalize; color:#d10000; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Express Shipping&lt;/storng&gt; on orders over {0}",
                    expedited_shipping: "&lt;storng style=&#34;text-transform: capitalize; color:#d10000; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Flat Rate Shipping&lt;/storng&gt; on orders over {0}",
                    stand_shipping: "&lt;storng style=&#34;text-transform: capitalize; color:#d10000; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Standard Shipping&lt;/storng&gt; on orders over {0}",
                    shop_transit: "free picking up at store for order over  {0}",
                  }
                  var textTpl1 = {
                    express_shipping: "&lt;storng style=&#34;text-transform: capitalize; color:#d10000; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Express Shipping!&lt;/storng&gt;",
                    expedited_shipping: "&lt;storng style=&#34;text-transform: capitalize; color:#f35b6e; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Flat Rate Shipping! &lt;/storng&gt;",
                    stand_shipping: "&lt;storng style=&#34;text-transform: capitalize; color:#d10000; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Standard Shipping! &lt;/storng&gt;",
                    shop_transit: "&lt;strong style=&#34;color:#f35b6e; font-weight:700&#34;&gt;Free Picking Up At Store!&lt;/strong&gt;",
                  }
                  shippingData.forEach(function(val) {
                      var text = SHEIN_W.htmlDecode(textTpl[val.type] ? textTpl[val.type] : textTpl['stand_shipping']);
                      var text1 = SHEIN_W.htmlDecode(textTpl1[val.type] ? textTpl1[val.type] : textTpl1['stand_shipping']);
                      var el1 = '<span>'+SHEIN_W.template(val.full_amount.amountWithSymbol, text)+'</span>';
                      var el2 = '<span>'+text1+'</span>';
                      var invoke = Number(val.full_amount.amount);
                      if(invoke > 0){
                          freeShippingTipsData.push(el1);
                      }else if(invoke == 0 && val.shippingPrices.amount == 0){
                          freeShippingTipsData.push(el2);
                      }
                  });
                  freeHTML  = freeShippingTipsData.map(function(tip, i) {
                      var hrefVal = "" + "/Shipping-Info-a-280.html";
                      return '<li class="discount"><a href='+hrefVal+'>'+tip+'</a></li>';
                  });
              }
              // 首单优惠数据
              if(data.freeShippingTips && data.freeShippingTips.length){
                  var freeShippingTips = data.freeShippingTips;
                  freeShippingTips.forEach(function(item) {
                      freeHTML.push('<li class="discount">' + item.replace(/http\:\/\/\w+.shein.\w+/gi, '') + '</li>');
                  });
              }

              $('.j-free-shipping').append(freeHTML.join(''))

              // free shipping 动画
              var index = 0,
                  stop = false,
                  num =  $('.j-free-shipping >li').length,
                  liEls = $('.j-free-shipping >li');

              function shippingflipInX(){
                  if(stop) return false;
                  if(index > (num-2)){
                    liEls.addClass('she-none');
                    liEls.removeClass('animated flipInX she-block');
                    index = 0;
                    liEls.eq(0).addClass('animated flipInX she-block').removeClass('she-none');
                    return;
                  }

                  liEls.addClass('she-none');
                  liEls.removeClass('animated flipInX she-block');
                  //下一个
                  // liEls.eq(index).addClass('none');
                  liEls.eq(index+1).removeClass('she-none').addClass('animated flipInX she-block');
                  index ++ ;
              }
              var hdtimer = setInterval(function(){
                  shippingflipInX();
              },3000);
              $('.j-free-shipping').hover(function(){
                stop = true;
              },function(){
                stop = false;
              })
          })
      });
    }
  }());
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  function getCookie(name){/*获取指定名称的cookie的值*/
      var value = "; " + document.cookie;
      var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
      if (parts.length >= 2) {
          return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
      } else {
          return undefined;
      }
    }
</script>

    <script>
    ; (function () {
        function setCookie(name, val, expires, domain) {
            //domain = domain || __CurrentMainDomain__;
            var text = String(encodeURIComponent(val));
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + Number(expires) * 1000);
            text += '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();
            // domain
            text += '; path=/';
            if (typeof (domain) != "undefined" && domain != "") {
                text += '; domain=' + __CurrentMainDomain__;
            }

            document.cookie = name + '=' + text;
        }

        function getCookie(name) {/*获取指定名称的cookie的值*/
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length >= 2) {
                return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
            } else {
                return undefined;
            }
        }

        function currencyAutoMatch(country) {
            //中东国家默认货币
            // 1.ar和mar站根据ip，匹配对应国家的币种，在用户后首次打开时即显示匹配后的币种。
            // 2.若用户已经保存有货币，则不需要重新判断和更改
            var currencyMap = {
                SA: 'SAR',
                AE: 'AED',
                KW: 'KWD',
                QA: 'QAR',
                OM: 'OMR',
                BH: 'BHD',
            }, site = 'us',
                currency = getCookie('m_currency_' + site)

            if ((site == 'ar') && !currency && country in currencyMap) {
                currency = currencyMap[country]
                $.get('/changeCurrency?currency=' + currency, function () {
                    setCookie('m_currency_' + site, currency, 60 * 60 * 24 * 7)
                    window.location.reload(true)
                })

			} else if (site == 'asia' && country ){
				var asiaCurrencyMap = {
					'us': 'USD',
					'sa': 'SAR',
					'kw': 'KWD',
					'sg': 'SGD',
					'qa': 'QAR',
					'om': 'OMR',
					'bh': 'BHD',
					'tw': 'TWD',
					'il': 'ILS',
					'th': 'THB',
					'id': 'IDR',
					'tr': 'TRY',
					'vn': 'VND',
					'hk': 'HKD',
					'ph': 'PHP'
				}

				var asiaCountry = country.toLowerCase()

				if( !SHEIN_W.getCookie('currency') && asiaCurrencyMap[asiaCountry]) {
					var asiaCurrency = asiaCurrencyMap[asiaCountry]
					$.get('/changeCurrency?currency=' + asiaCurrency, function () {
						window.location.reload(true)
					})
				}
			}
        }

        //cookie中countryId不存在并且是非国际站
        if( (getCookie('countryId') == undefined && 'us' != 'en') || (!getCookie('currency') && gbCommonInfo.lang == 'asia') ){
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: '/judgeIP',
                success: function (res) {
                    if (res.code != 0) return
                    var country = res.info.location.country;
                    var countryId = res.info.location.country_id;
                    setCookie('countryId', countryId, 3600 * 24 * 30, false)

                    currencyAutoMatch(country)
                }
            })
        }
    }())
</script>

<script>
    ! function (f, b, e, v, n, t, s) {
        if (f.fbq) return;
        n = f.fbq = function () {
            n.callMethod ?
                n.callMethod.apply(n, arguments) : n.queue.push(arguments)
        };
        if (!f._fbq) f._fbq = n;
        n.push = n;
        n.loaded = !0;
        n.version = '2.0';
        n.queue = [];
        t = b.createElement(e);
        t.async = !0;
        t.src = v;
        s = b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
        s.parentNode.insertBefore(t, s)
    }(window, document, 'script', 'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');

                appId : '312563225523989',
                // autoLogAppEvents : true,
                status: true,
                cookie: true,
                xfbml: true,

        (function (d, s, id) {
            var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
            if (d.getElementById(id)) {
                return;
            }
            js = d.createElement(s);
            js.id = id;
            js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js";
            fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
        }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
    


    window.doFbq = function (action, params) {
        ! function () {
            if (typeof Object.assign != 'function') {
                Object.assign = function (target) {
                    'use strict';
                    if (target == null) {
                        throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object');
                    }

                    target = Object(target);
                    for (var index = 1; index < arguments.length; index++) {
                        var source = arguments[index];
                        if (source != null) {
                            for (var key in source) {
                                if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, key)) {
                                    target[key] = source[key];
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    return target;
                };
            }
            if (typeof fbq !== 'undefined') {
                var _form = Object.assign({}, {
                    content_type: 'product', //直接上报此文本
                    value: 1.00, //固定上报此价格
                    currency: 'USD' //固定上报此币种
                }, params)

                if(typeof fbq.init !== 'function') {
                    var _timeIndex = 0;
                    var _timeId = setInterval(function() {
                        _timeIndex++;
                        if(typeof fbq.init == 'function' || _timeIndex>5) {
                            fbq('track', action, _form);
                            clearInterval(_timeId);
                        }
                    }, 1000);
                } else {
                    fbq('track', action, _form);
                }

            }
        }();
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" data-id="index-stylegallery-vue">
	Vue.component('index-stylegallery', {
	    template: '#index-stylegallery',
	    data: function() {
	    	return {
	    		goods: {},
          navData: [],
	    		status: { loading: -1, loginModal: false},
	    		quickOpenEvent: { status: { open: false } },
          language: "us",
          loginModal: {type: '', ref: null},
          forgetPassword: { showForm: false, },
          gaCache: {},
          added_wish: {},
          index: 0
	    	}
	    },
	    computed: {
        },
        watch: {
        },
        mounted: function() {
            this.bindEvent();
			if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
				GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
			}
        },
	    methods: {
	    	bindEvent: function() {
                var self = this;
                $( function(){
                    self.loadGoodsData();
                    self.getNavData();
                    }
                )

                $(window).scroll(function(e){
                    if(self.scrollTimeout){
                        clearTimeout(self.scrollTimeout);
                    }
                    self.scrollTimeout = setTimeout(self.sa_scrollHandler,500);
                });
	    	},
	    	loadGoodsData: function() {
	    		var self = this;
	    		// $.getJSON('//api-shein.shein.com/review/top_picks?p=1&callback=?', {language: 'us'}, function(data) {
                $.ajax({
                    url: '//api-shein.shein.com/social_wear/wear_list_pc?ps=10&callback=?',
                    type: 'get',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    jsonp: 'callback',
                    data: {
                        language: gbCalcSocialWearLang()
                    },
                    headers: {
                        SocialSiteFrom: 'pc'
                    },
                    success: function(data) {
                        if(data && data.info && data.info.wear_img_list && data.info.wear_img_list.length) {
                            self.goods = data.info.wear_img_list;
                            self.nextTick();
                            $('.outfit-container').css('visibility', 'visible');
                            $(window).scroll();
                        } else {
                            $('.outfit-container').hide();
                        }
                    }
			    });
	    	},
	    	// opt
            quickViewOpen: function(opt) {
              var self = this;
              this.index = opt.index
            	if(this.status.loading >= 0) return;
            	this.status.loading = opt.index;
                this.sa_clickPhoto(opt.goodsId,opt.index+1);
                this.quickOpenEvent = {
                    status: {
                        open: true,
                        pageType: 'home'
                    },
                    data: {
                        goodsId: opt.goodsId,
                        styleGalleryData: {
                            _oimg: opt.oimg || '',
                            _simg: opt.simg || '',
                            pageType: 'styleGallery-home'
                        },
                        index: opt.index,
                        activity_from: 'style_gallery',
                        code: 'styleGallery',
                        eventCategory: '推荐列表',
                        moduleName: 'recommend',
                        gaTitle: 'StyleGallery'
                    },
                    callback: function(data, code) {
                        self.quickOpenEvent.status.open = false
                        // self.quickOpenEvent = { status: { open: false } };
                    	self.status.loading = -1;
                    }
                }
            },
            qvAddWishSuc: function(goods_id) {
              if(this.added_wish[goods_id]) {
                this.$set(this.added_wish, goods_id, 0)
              } else {
                this.$set(this.added_wish, goods_id, 1)
              }
            },
            //DOM渲染完成后数据处理函数
            nextTick: function() {
            	var self = this;
            	var _prevButton = '.j-outfit-prev';
	            var _nextButton = '.j-outfit-next';

	            this.$nextTick(function () {
	            	self.outfitSwiper = new Swiper ('.j-outfit-swiper', {
		                direction: 'horizontal',
		                prevButton: _prevButton,
		                nextButton: _nextButton,
		                spaceBetween: 20,
		                slidesPerView: 5,
		                slidesPerGroup : 5,
		                lazyLoadingInPrevNext : true,
		                lazyLoading: true,
                        onSlideChangeEnd: function(swiper){
                            self.sa_exposePhotos();
                            if(typeof(gaEventCenter) != 'undefined') {
                                gaEventCenter.$emit('slideChangeEnd', {swiper: swiper})
                            }
							if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
			                    GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
			                }
                        },
                        onSlidePrevEnd: function(swiper){
                            if(typeof(gaEventCenter) != 'undefined') {
                                gaEventCenter.$emit('SlidePrevEnd')
                            }
                        },
                        onSlideNextEnd: function(swiper){
                            if(typeof(gaEventCenter) != 'undefined') {
                                gaEventCenter.$emit('SlideNextEnd')
                            }
                        }
		            });
					if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
						GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
					}
		        });
            },
            getNavData: function(times) {
                var self = this, navLoadFailTime = 0;
                if(times) navLoadFailTime = times;
                var navAjax = $.ajax({
                    // url: '//api-shein.shein.com/review/m/category',
                    url: '//api-shein.shein.com/social_wear/label_list_pc',
                    type: 'get',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    jsonp: 'callback',
                    timeout: 5000,
                    data: {
                        language: gbCalcSocialWearLang(),
                        label_type:1
                    },
                    headers: {
                        SocialSiteFrom: 'pc'
                    }
                })
                .done(function(data) {
                    if(data && data.code == 0 && data.info && data.info.category_list && data.info.category_list.length) {

                        self.navData = data.info.category_list;
                        self.$nextTick(function() {
                            new Swiper ('.j-tags-swiper', {
                                direction: 'horizontal',
                                prevButton: '.j-tags-prev',
                                nextButton: '.j-tags-next',
                                spaceBetween: 15,
                                slidesPerView: 'auto',
                                slidesPerGroup : 5,
                                onSlideChangeEnd: function(){
                                    self.sa_exposeMenu();
									if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
					                    GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
					                }
                                }
                            });
							if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
								GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
							}
                        })
                        $(window).scroll();
                    }
                })
                .fail(function() {
                    navLoadFailTime++;
                    if(navLoadFailTime < 5) {
                        self.getNavData(navLoadFailTime);
                    }
                })
            },
            clickNav: function(opt) {
                if(opt.url) {
                    window.location.href = opt.url;
                    this.sa_clickMenu(opt.labelId,opt.pitPos);
                }
            },
			// 登录弹框
			openLoginModal: function(cbType, cbRef) {
				this.status.loginModal = true;
				this.loginModal.type = cbType;
				this.loginModal.ref = cbRef;
			},
			loginModalSucCb: function() {
				this.status.loginModal = false;
				SHEIN_W.userModule.update_top_login();
				cart_module.reload();
				if (this.loginModal.type === 'qv-add-wish') {
					this.loginModal.ref.addToWish();
				}
			},
            loginModalClose: function() {
                this.status.loginModal = false
                window.LOGIN_GA_CLOSE_POPUPS_SEND({ scenes: 'wishlist' })
            },
            transformImg: transformImg,
            sa_scrollHandler:function(){
                //style gallery 曝光
                var stylegalleryMenu = $('.c-style-gallery-nav');
                if(!stylegalleryMenu.hasClass("sa_expose")){
                    if($(window).height() >= stylegalleryMenu.get(0).getBoundingClientRect().bottom * 0.8){
                        this.sa_exposeMenu();
                        this.sa_exposePhotos();
                        stylegalleryMenu.addClass('sa_expose');
                    }
                }
            },
            sa_exposeMenu:function(){
                var stylegalleryMenu = $('.c-style-gallery-nav');
                var clientRect = stylegalleryMenu.get(0).getBoundingClientRect();
                var param = '';
                var self = this;
                stylegalleryMenu.find('.swiper-slide').each(function(index,item){
                    var itemClientRect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
                    if(itemClientRect.left>=clientRect.left-20 && itemClientRect.right<=clientRect.right+20 && !$(item).hasClass('sa_expose')){
                        param += (index+1)+'`'+self.navData[index].label_id+',';
                        $(item).addClass('sa_expose');
                    }
                });
                if(param.length>0){
                    param = param.substring(0,param.length-1);
                    sa('send',{'activity_name':'expose_home_style_gallery_style','activity_param':{
                        content_list:param
                    }});
                }
            },
            sa_exposePhotos:function(){
                var stylegalleryPhotos = $('.c-style-gallery-nav').prev();
                var clientRect = stylegalleryPhotos.get(0).getBoundingClientRect();
                var param = '';
                var self = this;
                stylegalleryPhotos.find('.swiper-slide').each(function(index,item){
                    var itemClientRect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
                    if(itemClientRect.left>=clientRect.left-20 && itemClientRect.right<=clientRect.right+20 && !$(item).hasClass('sa_expose')){
                        param += (index+1)+'`'+self.goods[index].goods_id+',';
                        $(item).addClass('sa_expose');
                    }
                });
                if(param.length>0){
                    param = param.substring(0,param.length-1);
                    sa('send',{'activity_name':'expose_home_style_gallery_goods','activity_param':{
                        goods_list:param,
                    }});
                }
            },
            sa_clickPhoto:function(_goodId,_pitPos){
                sa('send',{'activity_name':'click_home_style_gallery_goods','activity_param':{
                    goods_list:_pitPos+'`'+_goodId,
                }});
            },
            sa_clickMenu:function(_labelId,_pitPos){
                if(typeof _labelId == 'undefined'){
                    _labelId = 0;
                    _pitPos = 1;
                }
                sa('send',{'activity_name':'click_home_style_gallery_style','activity_param':{content_list:_pitPos+'`'+_labelId}});
            }
	    }
	});
</script>
